And when the dislocation is in front, it must be stretched the bad leg quickly, as I have said; and put the pin to stay above the bad knee, then press with the other hand, and stretch downward toward the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches; et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table; et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz; adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve; et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus; et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors; puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And if the dislocation is on the side, it must not be stretched downward or lifted from the ground, but it should be positioned as if the hip were dislocated to the side, as we have said regarding lying on the two hips; and it should be held with a splint as we said before, and one hand should press at the joint. It will be right when the patient stretches his legs, and they are equal; then adjust the thighs, apply the plaster, and the bandage so that the hips do not move; and let it rest for three or four days, then release it, and apply the plaster again; and if you see that they are equal, hold it as before and let it rest for three days; then release it, and allow the hip to heal properly, until the limb is strengthened.
de la dislocation dou genoil	of the dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres: c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier; et ne desalue point devant.	The knee is dislocated in three ways: namely, internally and externally, and behind; and it does not dislocate in front.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez; et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez; puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment; et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement; et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie; et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And the signs are that you instruct the patient to bend their leg at the thigh, and if it does not fit against the thigh, know that it is dislocated; and for the restoration of all this, you make the patient sit upright, extend their leg if possible, and place your back against their thigh, putting their foot on yours. Then take their knee with your palms, pull it gently between your hands, and form the two sides of the knee properly. Have other attendants extend their foot until the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that the leg fits easily against the thigh; then apply the plaster and heat the leg to the thigh, binding them tightly for three or four days, after which you release the bindings. The patient should not move much during this time until the limb is strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not in place, administer strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	of the ankle dislocation
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The ankle is sometimes injured, and sometimes fully dislocated, both inside and out.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee: li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	And the signs are that the ankle is swollen, and protrudes forward to the part where it is dislocated: the correction is slight, and one should gently extend it with their hands when it is only injured.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	And when it is fully dislocated, you must seat the patient upright, and hold them by the ministers outside the leg, above the ankle; then pull the foot towards your right hand, and twice to your left hand, then extend it upwards, and firmly place the foot at the top; do this twice as we have said, by pulling and pulling the foot; if it returns, that is well; if not, restart the procedure, for it will return; and if it cannot return in this way, let the patient lie on their back on the ground, and drive the stake firmly into the earth between their thighs, and tie cords tightly around them to prevent the patient from moving; then hold the thigh of the healthy leg beneath, and another minister extend the foot at their hands or at the ankle, tying it above the foot's neck; then equally extend each minister, and the stake should be placed firmly between the patient’s thighs to keep the patient from moving when they are extended; then place your fingers evenly on the dislocation at your hands, and another minister hold the healthy leg below, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And when it is at point, put the plaster and stops on, strain forment, and tie the foot to the leg, and guard the nerves that are above the ankle behind, that the ligatures not be too tight; then let it for two days or three, and as the ligatures mollify, so unbind; then release at the third day or the fourth, and defend going the patient for four days; and if he goes before this term, it is not safety that he does not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if abscesses chase away, it is necessary that you appease them, as we have said elsewhere, while they are diseased.
des dois	of the two
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the two are dislocated, it is necessary to extend them beautifully with effort, and this is a light matter.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the dislocation is in any part of the back or foot, you must make the patient sit on a plain seat or on a chair completely upright, and place their foot over what appears to be the joint. Then press firmly on their foot until it returns to its proper position; and when it is equal and nothing appears amiss, put a stool under the sole of the foot, then hold firm, and let them rest for three days, after which you release it; and make it rest until it is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	Of wounds and dislocations together.
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	When a wound comes with dislocation, and one sees hope for its restoration, many times the patient dies: so do not be overly presumptuous in the treatment, if you are not skilled in the art and have not used it long, and if you are not always pitiful and merciful and slow; but at the beginning use calming treatments for hot abscesses, and leave the patient to God, if you see no hope of recovery; and when you see hope, now reset the limb to its place, as the abscesses die away. And when the limb is in place, administer calming treatments for hot abscesses, and treat the wound as it should be with drying ointments; and if there is dislocation with fracture and small broken bones, extract them, and do what we have said in simple diseases; and guard against entering a path of fear, according to what I have said, for this benefits you according to your Creator, and for the knowledge that arms you and your body.
Amen	Amen
